Jay Leno:

"Today, the House approved drilling in Alaska's National Wildlife Refuge. . This has divided the country, but this points out the differences between our major political parties. See, the Republicans drill wherever they want, the Democrats drill whoever they want."

Jay Leno:

"Oh, California Senator Dianne Feinstein -- woo! Was she mad today. Did you hear about this? She's furious at Gary Condit. She says she cannot forgive Gary Condit for lying to her. I guess he told her he didn't have an affair. She said she can't forgive him and there's nothing he can do. And Condit said today that's okay that she's mad at him right now 'cause he said, 'You know, makeup sex, that's the best thing.'"

Jay Leno:

"President Bush's choice to run the FBI, Robert Mueller, testifying before the Senate Judiciary Committee. They needed a new FBI chief because, as you know, they misplaced the old one."

Jay Leno:

"President Bush does not do well with African Americans, but he's trying. He promised the Urban League today that if they support his education reform plan, he'll try -- let me emphasize this -- he will try and make sure the ballots of black people will actually be counted in the next election."

Jay Leno:

"A blue ribbon panel headed by former Presidents Jimmy Carter and Gerald Ford came up with a list of ways to improve our next presidential election. Are these the best guys for the job? Ford and Carter? I mean, between the two of them, they could only win one election, you know?"

Jay Leno:

"And William Kennedy-Smith -- remember him? He was acquitted of sexual assault charges in that sensational trial. . He said no to becoming a US congressman. Earlier in the week, he said he might run for Congress, but now he says no. But then again, with him, no might not always mean no."

Jay Leno:

"Florida Secretary of State Katherine 'Cruella de Vil' Harris -- you know her. She's running for Congress, now being investigated for budgeting $3.5 million for overseas travel. $3.5 million? How does she spend so much money on travel? Couldn't she just hop on her broom when she wanted to go somewhere?"

Jay Leno:

"Bill Clinton getting $8 million for his memoirs. Isn't that unbelievable? In fact, the publisher said today it would have been $10 million if Clinton had agreed to tell the truth, but good luck with that."

Jay Leno:

"According to a new medical study released today, beer may actually be good for your heart. You know what that means? If Jenna Bush would just give her beer to Dick Cheney, we could take care of two problems at the same time."

David Letterman:

"Things are back to normal for former President Clinton, he's now in his office building up there in Harlem, and it's a fantastic, brand new. Yeah, sure. Fantastic new office. He's got, like, a 360-degree view, which is great. He can see Hillary coming from any direction."

David Letterman:

"He's got the staff, he's got the big office, and, you know, too bad he doesn't have a job. So he sits around in his office and, honestly, he's got nothing to do. For example, earlier today, you know, to kill a little time, he Xeroxed his ass, and then he faxed it to Carmen Electra."

David Letterman:

"But don't kid yourself. They're busy up there. They say on any given day, they'll have as many as up to, like a dozen people in the reception area, or as it's also known, his lap."

"And President Bush announced that he's gonna be away from the White House, taking the entire month of August off. Wow, who among us hasn't needed 30 straight days off after working 6 whole months? Woo! Take a break."

Jay Leno:

"Why is Bush taking a break? Cheney's the guy that needs time off. Huh? The man's had 18 heart attacks in 13 weeks. Give the man a break."

Jay Leno:

"I guess you heard the prosecution has reached a plea-bargain agreement in that racketeering case against the Atlanta Gold Club. Under the terms of agreement, the Federal Government will take control of the strip club. How frustrating is that for Bill Clinton?"

Jay Leno:

"Think about this. Eight years in the White House, and the Federal Government gets its very own strip club only six months after he leaves office. He could have been commissioner of lap dances, do you realize that?"

Jay Leno:

"The other day, with much fanfare, President Clinton opened his new office in Harlem. And the word is well, President Bush a little jealous of all the attention Clinton was getting. In fact, now there's talk that Bush might want his own office in the White House, too."

Jay Leno:

"You know, Clinton's got this office, it's 7,000 square feet, beautiful -- he's got no job. The man doesn't know what to do with himself. In fact, Clinton was so bored yesterday, he actually called just to chat with Hillary."

Jay Leno:

"Former Vice President Al Gore has grown a beard. Did you see him on the news today? He didn't want to grow a beard. It's just after he lost to George Bush, his doctors took away any sharp objects."

Jay Leno:

"But God bless Al Gore. He's bounced back. . Look at this -- he got a new job. He's now the Brawny paper towel guy."

Jay Leno:

"For the past few days, Congress has been debating the ethics of cloning. And for many in Congress, this is their first experience with the subject -- not cloning, ethics."

Jay Leno:

"I guess the House finally approved a bill that would ban all forms of human cloning. The bill claims that human cloning is an irresponsible use of human DNA. And believe me, if there's anybody that knows about irresponsible use of human DNA, it's our US Congress."

Jay Leno:

"The Pentagon announced today plans to let Kentucky Fried Chicken and Dunkin' Donuts provide food for our troops. What was the thinking behind this, huh? What, were our soldiers gettin' through the obstacle course a little too quickly?"

Jay Leno:

"When you think about it, does Kentucky Fried Chicken even want to get involved with the Pentagon? The Colonel's secret recipe, will be in Chinese hands within 24 hours."

"Here's good news. The House has approved drilling for oil in the Alaska wilderness. Say what you will about Clinton, but he was only interested in drilling in the Oval Office."

David Letterman:

"Hillary Clinton, our senator, got her first bill passed - a ban on cock fighting in New York. . Remember when she was running for the office, people said she would not listen to the concerns of New Yorkers? Well. . And now that cockfighting has been outlawed, New Yorkers got nothing to do."

Jay Leno:

"I'm glad our President is in perfect health, but it's not the same excitement as when Clinton would go in for a physical. Because with Clinton, there would always be, like, five or six urologists there, you know. You never know what strange disease he might have picked up. 'More penicillin! We need backup! More penicillin!'"

Jay Leno:

"President Bush taking the entire month of August off. This is what he said. Bush said today he thinks it is important for a president to spend time away from Washington, or at least that's what Dick Cheney told him."

Jay Leno:

"Actually, Vice President Cheney is also on vacation. He's in Jackson Hole, Wyoming. What a better place for a guy who's had four heart attacks. He's in a place with thin air, rugged hiking and all-beef dinners. Why don't you get him some snow to shovel while he's out there, too?"

Jay Leno:

"Isn't this unbelievable? I mean, all of Washington is shut down. Congress is in recess. Bush is gone. Cheney is gone. In fact, it is so lonely in DC now, the NRA and the tobacco companies just handed money to each other."

"Al Gore has returned to the United States after a long vacation in Europe. Did you know he was gone? Vacation from what?"
